A moray eel uses a second set of jaws in the back of its throat to snatch prey. The octopus camouflages itself until a helpless victim wanders to close.\n\nClick here for more documentaries: http://bit.ly/2gSPaf6\n\nFollow us on Facebook: facebook.com/realwildschannel\n\nFollow us on Instagram: https://www.instagram.com/realwildchannel/\n\nAny queries, please contact us at: owned-enquiries@littledotstudios.com\n\nContent licensed from Earth Touch to Little Dot Studios.
